\subsubsection{Merge All Covariate Layers}\label{merge-all-covariate-layers}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Merge covariates and climate data}
\NormalTok{cov.dat }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(cov.dat, newhall, temperatureRegime, moistureRegime)}
    
\CommentTok{\# Project if necessary}
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{crs}\NormalTok{(cov.dat) }\SpecialCharTok{!=}\NormalTok{ epsg) \{}
\NormalTok{  cov.dat }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ terra}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{project}\NormalTok{(cov.dat, epsg, }\AttributeTok{method =} \StringTok{"near"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\CommentTok{\# Add geology if exists}
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{exists}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"geo"}\NormalTok{)) \{}
\NormalTok{  geo }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rasterize}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as}\NormalTok{(geo, }\StringTok{"SpatVector"}\NormalTok{), cov.dat, }\AttributeTok{field =} \StringTok{"GEO"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  geo }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{dummies}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{ca.rast =}\NormalTok{ geo}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{GEO, }\AttributeTok{preval =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{absval =} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  cov.dat }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(cov.dat, geo)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\CommentTok{\# Add geomorphology if exists}
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{exists}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"geomorph"}\NormalTok{)) \{}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{inherits}\NormalTok{(geomorph, }\StringTok{"SpatRaster"}\NormalTok{)) \{}
\NormalTok{    geomorph }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rasterize}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as}\NormalTok{(geomorph, }\StringTok{"SpatVector"}\NormalTok{), cov.dat, }\AttributeTok{field =} \StringTok{"GEOMORPH"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
\NormalTok{  geomorph }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{dummies}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{ca.rast =}\NormalTok{ geomorph}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{GEOMORPH, }\AttributeTok{preval =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{absval =} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Ensure matching extent and resolution}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{identical}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{ext}\NormalTok{(cov.dat), }\FunctionTok{ext}\NormalTok{(geomorph))) \{}
\NormalTok{    geomorph }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{extend}\NormalTok{(geomorph, cov.dat)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{all}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{res}\NormalTok{(cov.dat) }\SpecialCharTok{==} \FunctionTok{res}\NormalTok{(geomorph))) \{}
\NormalTok{    geomorph }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{resample}\NormalTok{(geomorph, cov.dat, }\AttributeTok{method =} \StringTok{"near"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  
\NormalTok{  cov.dat }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(cov.dat, geomorph)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\CommentTok{\# Cleanup}
\FunctionTok{rm}\NormalTok{(newhall, geomorph, geo)}
\FunctionTok{gc}\NormalTok{()}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{Final covariate stack: \%d layers}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nlyr}\NormalTok{(cov.dat)))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{quote}
\textbf{💡 Note}: \textbf{Stacking} is the process of combining multiple spatial data layers (raster datasets) into a single multi-layer object. This is useful when multiple variables need to be analyzed together.
\end{quote}

\subsection{Principal Component Analysis (PCA)}\label{pca}

PCA reduces dimensionality while retaining the most important information. Components explaining 99\% of variance are kept.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Perform PCA}
\NormalTok{pca }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ synoptReg}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{raster\_pca}\NormalTok{(cov.dat)  }\CommentTok{\# Faster than terra::princomp}

\CommentTok{\# Get SpatRaster layers}
\NormalTok{cov.dat }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ pca}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{PCA}

\CommentTok{\# Display summary}
\FunctionTok{summary}\NormalTok{(cov.dat)}

\CommentTok{\# Subset to main PCs (variance explained \textgreater{}= 0.99)}
\NormalTok{n\_comps }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{first}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{which}\NormalTok{(pca}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{summaryPCA[}\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{,] }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \FloatTok{0.99}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{cov.dat }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ pca}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{PCA[[}\DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{:}\NormalTok{n\_comps]]}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{Retained \%d principal components (99\%\% variance)}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, n\_comps))}

\CommentTok{\# Save PCA rasters}
\FunctionTok{writeRaster}\NormalTok{(cov.dat, }
            \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(results.path, }\StringTok{"PCA\_projected.tif"}\NormalTok{), }
            \AttributeTok{overwrite =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Cleanup}
\FunctionTok{rm}\NormalTok{(pca)}

\CommentTok{\# Reload if needed}
\CommentTok{\# cov.dat \textless{}{-} rast(paste0(results.path, "PCA\_projected.tif"))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsubsection{Aggregate to 100m Resolution}\label{aggregate-to-100m-resolution}

\CommentTok{\# Display new resolution}
\NormalTok{lu}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsubsection{Filter Legacy Data}\label{filter-legacy-data}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{exists}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"legacy"}\NormalTok{)) \{}
  \CommentTok{\# Keep only legacy points within land{-}use areas}
\NormalTok{  legacy}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{INSIDE }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ terra}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{extract}\NormalTok{(crops, legacy) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}\NormalTok{ dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(lu)}
\NormalTok{  legacy }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ legacy[}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(legacy}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{INSIDE), ] }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
\NormalTok{    dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\StringTok{"INSIDE"}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Legacy points within land{-}use areas: \%d}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(legacy)))}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\FunctionTok{rm}\NormalTok{(extracted\_values)}

\end{Highlighting}

\subsection{Rasterize PSUs for Covariate Space Coverage}\label{rasterize-psus}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Create raster template at PSU resolution}
\NormalTok{template }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rast}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{vect}\NormalTok{(psu\_grid\_filtered), }\AttributeTok{res =}\NormalTok{ psu\_size)}
\NormalTok{template }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rasterize}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{vect}\NormalTok{(psu\_grid\_filtered), template, }\AttributeTok{field =} \StringTok{"ID"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Crop covariates to filtered PSUs}
\NormalTok{cov.dat }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{crop}\NormalTok{(cov.dat, psu\_grid\_filtered, }\AttributeTok{mask =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{overwrite =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Resample covariates to match PSU template}
\NormalTok{PSU.r }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{resample}\NormalTok{(cov.dat, template)}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Covariates resampled to PSU resolution}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{quote}
\textbf{💡 Why this matters}: Cropping and resampling ensure that spatial resolution and extent of covariates match the PSU grid, facilitating accurate clustering.
\end{quote}

\subsection{Compute Optimal Sample Size}\label{optimal-sample-size}

After rasterizing PSUs for Covariate Space Coverage, calculate the optimal sample size based on divergence metrics (\citeproc{ref-saurette2023}{Saurette \emph{et al.}, 2023}).

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Load optimization script}
\FunctionTok{source}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"scripts/opt\_sample.R"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Prepare covariate data}
\NormalTok{psu.r.df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(PSU.r)}

\CommentTok{\# Define parameters}
\NormalTok{initial.n }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{50}     \CommentTok{\# Minimum sample size}
\NormalTok{final.n }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{3000}     \CommentTok{\# Maximum sample size}
\NormalTok{by.n }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{25}          \CommentTok{\# Increment step}
\NormalTok{iters }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{4}          \CommentTok{\# Iterations per trial}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsubsection{Run Optimization}\label{run-optimization}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Calculate optimal sample size using normalized KL{-}divergence}
\NormalTok{opt\_N\_fcs }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{opt\_sample}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{alg =} \StringTok{"fcs"}\NormalTok{,              }\CommentTok{\# Feature coverage sampling}
  \AttributeTok{s\_min =}\NormalTok{ initial.n, }
  \AttributeTok{s\_max =}\NormalTok{ final.n, }
  \AttributeTok{s\_step =}\NormalTok{ by.n, }
  \AttributeTok{s\_reps =}\NormalTok{ iters, }
  \AttributeTok{covs =}\NormalTok{ psu.r.df, }
  \AttributeTok{cpus =} \ConstantTok{NULL}\NormalTok{,              }\CommentTok{\# Use all available cores}
  \AttributeTok{conf =} \FloatTok{0.95}
\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Display results}
\FunctionTok{print}\NormalTok{(opt\_N\_fcs}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{optimal\_sites)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsubsection{Extract Optimal Sample Size}\label{extract-optimal-sample-size}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Use Kullback{-}Leibler Divergence (most reliable)}
\NormalTok{optimal\_N\_KLD }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ opt\_N\_fcs}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{optimal\_sites[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{]}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{✓ Optimal sample size: \%d PSUs}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, optimal\_N\_KLD))}

\CommentTok{\# Set final PSU count}
\NormalTok{n.psu }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ optimal\_N\_KLD}

\CommentTok{\# Expected total sampling sites (4 per PSU)}
\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Expected total target sites: \%d}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, n.psu }\SpecialCharTok{*} \DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{quote}
\textbf{💡 Note}: The optimal sample size is based on Kullback-Leibler Divergence, which does not overestimate like Jensen-Shannon methods.
\end{quote}

\subsection{Covariate Space Coverage - Computing PSUs}\label{csc-computing}

Covariate Space Coverage (CSC) sampling ensures sampling units are distributed effectively across the multidimensional space of environmental covariates.

\subsubsection{Prepare Function Parameters}\label{prepare-function-parameters}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Convert raster to dataframe with coordinates}
\NormalTok{PSU.df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{as.data.frame}\NormalTok{(PSU.r, }\AttributeTok{xy =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Get covariate names}
\NormalTok{covs }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(cov.dat)}

\CommentTok{\# Scale covariates (mean = 0, SD = 1)}
\NormalTok{mygrd }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{scale}\NormalTok{(PSU.df[, covs]))}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Prepared \%d PSUs with \%d covariates for clustering}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }
            \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(mygrd), }\FunctionTok{ncol}\NormalTok{(mygrd)))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsubsection{Perform K-means Clustering}\label{perform-k-means-clustering}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# With legacy data}
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{exists}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"legacy"}\NormalTok{)) \{}
  \CommentTok{\# Filter legacy to PSU grid extent}
\NormalTok{  legacy }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{st\_filter}\NormalTok{(legacy, psu\_grid\_filtered)}
\NormalTok{  legacy\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{st\_coordinates}\NormalTok{(legacy)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Find nearest PSU for each legacy point}
\NormalTok{  units }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{numeric}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(legacy\_df))}
  \ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ (i }\ControlFlowTok{in} \DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{:}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(legacy\_df)) \{}
\NormalTok{    distances }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sqrt}\NormalTok{((PSU.df}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{x }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ legacy\_df[i, }\StringTok{"X"}\NormalTok{])}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2} \SpecialCharTok{+} 
\NormalTok{                     (PSU.df}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ legacy\_df[i, }\StringTok{"Y"}\NormalTok{])}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    units[i] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{which.min}\NormalTok{(distances)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Create fixed centers from legacy points}
\NormalTok{  fixed }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{unique}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(units, }\FunctionTok{scale}\NormalTok{(PSU.df[, covs])[units, ]))}
  
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Incorporating \%d legacy points as fixed centers}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(fixed)))}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Run constrained clustering}
\NormalTok{  res }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{CSIS}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{fixed =}\NormalTok{ fixed, }
              \AttributeTok{nsup =}\NormalTok{ n.psu, }
              \AttributeTok{nstarts =}\NormalTok{ iterations, }
              \AttributeTok{mygrd =}\NormalTok{ mygrd)}
  
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
  \CommentTok{\# Standard k{-}means without legacy data}
\NormalTok{  res }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{kmeans}\NormalTok{(mygrd, }
                \AttributeTok{centers =}\NormalTok{ n.psu, }
                \AttributeTok{iter.max =} \DecValTok{10000}\NormalTok{, }
                \AttributeTok{nstart =} \DecValTok{100}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Running standard k{-}means with \%d centers}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, n.psu))}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{quote}
\textbf{💡 Note}: Progress is printed as ``X out of Y'' for each clustering iteration.
\end{quote}

\subsubsection{Assign Clusters and Calculate Distances}\label{assign-clusters-and-calculate-distances}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Assign clusters to PSUs}
\NormalTok{PSU.df}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ res}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster}

\CommentTok{\# Compute distances to nearest cluster center}
\NormalTok{D }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rdist}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{x1 =}\NormalTok{ res}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{centers, }\AttributeTok{x2 =} \FunctionTok{scale}\NormalTok{(PSU.df[, covs]))}
\NormalTok{units }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{apply}\NormalTok{(D, }\AttributeTok{MARGIN =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{FUN =}\NormalTok{ which.min)}

\CommentTok{\# Calculate Mean Squared Shortest Distance (MSSSD)}
\NormalTok{dmin }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{apply}\NormalTok{(D, }\AttributeTok{MARGIN =} \DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{, min)}
\NormalTok{MSSSD }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(dmin}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"MSSSD: \%.6f}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, MSSSD))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsubsection{Extract Selected PSUs}\label{extract-selected-psus}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Get selected PSU coordinates and covariates}
\NormalTok{myCSCsample }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ PSU.df[units, }\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"x"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"y"}\NormalTok{, covs)]}

\CommentTok{\# Label as legacy or new}
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{exists}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"legacy"}\NormalTok{)) \{}
\NormalTok{  myCSCsample}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{type }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{rep}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"legacy"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(fixed)), }
                        \FunctionTok{rep}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"new"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(units) }\SpecialCharTok{{-}} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(fixed)))}
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
\NormalTok{  myCSCsample}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{type }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"new"}
\NormalTok{\}}

\CommentTok{\# Convert to spatial object}
\NormalTok{myCSCsample }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ myCSCsample }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{st\_as\_sf}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{coords =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"x"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"y"}\NormalTok{), }\AttributeTok{crs =}\NormalTok{ epsg)}

\CommentTok{\# Separate legacy and new points}
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{exists}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"legacy"}\NormalTok{)) \{}
\NormalTok{  legacy }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ myCSCsample[myCSCsample}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{type }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"legacy"}\NormalTok{, ]}
\NormalTok{\}}
\NormalTok{new }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ myCSCsample[myCSCsample}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{type }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"new"}\NormalTok{, ]}

\CommentTok{\# Get PSU IDs}
\NormalTok{PSUs }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ sf}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{st\_intersection}\NormalTok{(psu\_grid\_filtered, new) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
\NormalTok{  dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(ID)}

\CommentTok{\# Extract target PSUs}
\NormalTok{target.PSUs }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ psu\_grid\_filtered[psu\_grid\_filtered}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{ID }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%}\NormalTok{ PSUs}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{ID, ] }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
\NormalTok{  dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(ID)}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{✓ Selected \%d target PSUs}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(target.PSUs)))}

\CommentTok{\# Cleanup}
\FunctionTok{rm}\NormalTok{(new, dmin, MSSSD)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsubsection{Visualize in Covariate Space}\label{visualize-in-covariate-space}

\subsection{Compute SSUs and TSUs}\label{compute-ssu-tsu}

Now we generate Secondary Sampling Units (100m × 100m) within each PSU and Tertiary Sampling Units (20m × 20m points) within each SSU.

\subsubsection{Load High-Resolution Covariates}\label{load-high-resolution-covariates}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Load SSU{-}level covariates (100m resolution)}
\NormalTok{cov.dat.ssu }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ terra}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{rast}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(raster.path, }
                                   \StringTok{"hres\_data/covs\_stack\_ssu\_1ha\_ZMB.tif"}\NormalTok{))}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Loaded \%d high{-}resolution covariates}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nlyr}\NormalTok{(cov.dat.ssu)))}

\CommentTok{\# Display covariate names}
\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(cov.dat.ssu)}

\CommentTok{\# Remove system{-}specific bands if needed}
\NormalTok{cov.dat.ssu }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{subset}\NormalTok{(cov.dat.ssu, }
                      \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(cov.dat.ssu)[}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(cov.dat.ssu) }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} 
                        \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"sysisen\_B2"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"sysisen\_B3"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"sysisen\_B4"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"sysisen\_B5"}\NormalTok{,}
                          \StringTok{"sysisen\_B6"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"sysisen\_B7"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"sysisen\_B8"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"sysisen\_B8A"}\NormalTok{,}
                          \StringTok{"sysisen\_B11"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"sysisen\_B12"}\NormalTok{)])}

\CommentTok{\# Replace NA with 0 (for categorical variables)}
\NormalTok{cov.dat.ssu[}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(cov.dat.ssu)] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{0}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Final SSU covariates: \%d layers}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nlyr}\NormalTok{(cov.dat.ssu)))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsubsection{Process Each PSU}\label{process-each-psu}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Initialize storage lists}
\NormalTok{selected\_ssus }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{()}
\NormalTok{all\_psus\_tsus }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{()}

\CommentTok{\# Main loop: Process each PSU}
\ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ (psu\_id }\ControlFlowTok{in} \DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{:}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(target.PSUs)) \{}
  
\NormalTok{  selected\_psu }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ target.PSUs[psu\_id, ]}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Generate 100m × 100m SSU grid}
\NormalTok{  ssu\_grid }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{st\_make\_grid}\NormalTok{(selected\_psu, }
                           \AttributeTok{cellsize =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(ssu\_size, ssu\_size), }
                           \AttributeTok{square =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  ssu\_grid\_sf }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{st\_sf}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{geometry =}\NormalTok{ ssu\_grid)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Convert to SpatVector for extraction}
\NormalTok{  ssu\_grid\_vect }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{vect}\NormalTok{(ssu\_grid\_sf)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Extract land{-}use values to filter SSUs}
\NormalTok{  extracted\_values }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{extract}\NormalTok{(crops, ssu\_grid\_vect, }\AttributeTok{fun =}\NormalTok{ table)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Calculate land{-}use percentage (25 pixels per SSU at 20m resolution)}
\NormalTok{  ssu\_grid\_sf}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{lu }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ (extracted\_values[, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{] }\SpecialCharTok{*} \DecValTok{100}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{/} \DecValTok{25}
\NormalTok{  ssu\_grid\_sf }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ ssu\_grid\_sf[ssu\_grid\_sf}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{lu }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}}\NormalTok{ percent\_crop, ]}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Progress update}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (psu\_id }\SpecialCharTok{\%\%} \DecValTok{10} \SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{0} \SpecialCharTok{||}\NormalTok{ psu\_id }\SpecialCharTok{==} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(target.PSUs)) \{}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}r}\StringTok{Progress: \%.2f\%\% (\%d out of \%d)"}\NormalTok{, }
\NormalTok{                (psu\_id }\SpecialCharTok{/} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(target.PSUs)) }\SpecialCharTok{*} \DecValTok{100}\NormalTok{, }
\NormalTok{                psu\_id, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(target.PSUs)))}
    \FunctionTok{flush.console}\NormalTok{()}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Check minimum SSU requirement}
\NormalTok{  total\_ssus }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(ssu\_grid\_sf)}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (total\_ssus }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}}\NormalTok{ (num\_primary\_ssus }\SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ num\_alternative\_ssus)) \{}
    \FunctionTok{warning}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"PSU"}\NormalTok{, psu\_id, }\StringTok{"does not have enough SSUs. Skipping."}\NormalTok{))}
    \ControlFlowTok{next}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Extract covariate values for each SSU}
\NormalTok{  ssu\_covariates }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ terra}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{extract}\NormalTok{(cov.dat.ssu, }\FunctionTok{vect}\NormalTok{(ssu\_grid\_sf), }\AttributeTok{df =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Merge with SSU spatial data}
\NormalTok{  ssu\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{cbind}\NormalTok{(ssu\_grid\_sf, ssu\_covariates[, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{])}
\NormalTok{  ssu\_data\_values }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{st\_drop\_geometry}\NormalTok{(ssu\_data)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Identify columns to exclude from scaling (categorical)}
\NormalTok{  exclude }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{grep}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\^{}geomorph\_|\^{}lu$"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(ssu\_data\_values), }\AttributeTok{value =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Separate scalable and non{-}scalable data}
\NormalTok{  to\_scale }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ ssu\_data\_values[, }\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(ssu\_data\_values) }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%}\NormalTok{ exclude]}
\NormalTok{  to\_keep  }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ ssu\_data\_values[, }\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(ssu\_data\_values) }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%}\NormalTok{ exclude, drop }\OtherTok{=} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{]}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Remove NA{-}only columns}
\NormalTok{  to\_scale }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ to\_scale[, }\FunctionTok{colSums}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(to\_scale)) }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, drop }\OtherTok{=} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{]}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Identify zero{-}variance columns}
\NormalTok{  zero\_variance\_cols }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sapply}\NormalTok{(to\_scale, }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(x) }\FunctionTok{sd}\NormalTok{(x, }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  zero\_variance\_cols[}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(zero\_variance\_cols)] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Scale only non{-}zero{-}variance columns}
\NormalTok{  scaled\_part }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ to\_scale}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{any}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{!}\NormalTok{zero\_variance\_cols)) \{}
\NormalTok{    scaled\_part[, }\SpecialCharTok{!}\NormalTok{zero\_variance\_cols] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{scale}\NormalTok{(to\_scale[, }\SpecialCharTok{!}\NormalTok{zero\_variance\_cols])}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Recombine}
\NormalTok{  mygrd\_ssu }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{cbind}\NormalTok{(to\_keep, scaled\_part)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Perform k{-}means clustering for this PSU}
\NormalTok{  optimal\_k }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ num\_primary\_ssus  }\CommentTok{\# 4 clusters}
\NormalTok{  kmeans\_result }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{kmeans}\NormalTok{(mygrd\_ssu[, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }
                          \AttributeTok{centers =}\NormalTok{ optimal\_k, }
                          \AttributeTok{iter.max =} \DecValTok{10000}\NormalTok{, }
                          \AttributeTok{nstart =} \DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{)}
  
\NormalTok{  ssu\_data}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{as.factor}\NormalTok{(kmeans\_result}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# CSC Sampling: Select closest SSUs to cluster centers}
\NormalTok{  D }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rdist}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{x1 =}\NormalTok{ kmeans\_result}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{centers, }\AttributeTok{x2 =}\NormalTok{ mygrd\_ssu[, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{])}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Target SSUs (closest to centers)}
\NormalTok{  target\_units }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{apply}\NormalTok{(D, }\AttributeTok{MARGIN =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{FUN =} \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(x) }\FunctionTok{order}\NormalTok{(x)[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{])}
\NormalTok{  target\_ssus }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ ssu\_data[target\_units, ]}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Replacement SSUs (second closest to centers)}
\NormalTok{  replacement\_units }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{apply}\NormalTok{(D, }\AttributeTok{MARGIN =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{FUN =} \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(x) }\FunctionTok{order}\NormalTok{(x)[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{])}
\NormalTok{  replacement\_ssus }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ ssu\_data[replacement\_units, ]}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Add metadata}
\NormalTok{  target\_ssus}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{SSU\_Type }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"Target"}
\NormalTok{  replacement\_ssus}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{SSU\_Type }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"Replacement"}
  
\NormalTok{  target\_ssus}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{SSU\_ID }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{:}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(target\_ssus)}
\NormalTok{  replacement\_ssus}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{SSU\_ID }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(target\_ssus) }\SpecialCharTok{+} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}\SpecialCharTok{:}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{2} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(target\_ssus))}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Link replacements to targets by cluster}
\NormalTok{  replacement\_ssus}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{replacement\_for }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sapply}\NormalTok{(replacement\_ssus}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster, }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(cl) \{}
\NormalTok{    matched }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ target\_ssus}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{SSU\_ID[target\_ssus}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster }\SpecialCharTok{==}\NormalTok{ cl]}
    \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(matched) }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{) }\FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(matched[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]) }\ControlFlowTok{else} \FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\ConstantTok{NA}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \})}
\NormalTok{  target\_ssus}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{replacement\_for }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ConstantTok{NA}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Add PSU ID}
\NormalTok{  target\_ssus}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{PSU\_ID }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selected\_psu}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{ID}
\NormalTok{  replacement\_ssus}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{PSU\_ID }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selected\_psu}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{ID}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Store SSUs}
\NormalTok{  selected\_ssus[[psu\_id]] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rbind}\NormalTok{(target\_ssus, replacement\_ssus)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Generate TSUs for target SSUs}
\NormalTok{  primary\_tsus }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{rownames}\NormalTok{(target\_ssus), }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(index) \{}
    \FunctionTok{generate\_tsu\_points\_within\_ssu}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{      ssu\_grid\_sf[}\FunctionTok{rownames}\NormalTok{(ssu\_grid\_sf) }\SpecialCharTok{==}\NormalTok{ index, ], }
\NormalTok{      number\_TSUs, }
\NormalTok{      index, }
      \StringTok{"Target"}\NormalTok{, }
\NormalTok{      crops}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  \})}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Generate TSUs for replacement SSUs}
\NormalTok{  alternative\_tsus }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{rownames}\NormalTok{(replacement\_ssus), }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(index) \{}
    \FunctionTok{generate\_tsu\_points\_within\_ssu}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{      ssu\_grid\_sf[}\FunctionTok{rownames}\NormalTok{(ssu\_grid\_sf) }\SpecialCharTok{==}\NormalTok{ index, ], }
\NormalTok{      number\_TSUs, }
\NormalTok{      index, }
      \StringTok{"Replacement"}\NormalTok{, }
\NormalTok{      crops}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  \})}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Combine all TSUs for this PSU}
\NormalTok{  all\_psus\_tsus[[psu\_id]] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{do.call}\NormalTok{(rbind, }\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(primary\_tsus, alternative\_tsus))}
\NormalTok{\}}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{✓ Processing complete}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"  Successful PSUs: \%d}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(selected\_ssus)))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsubsection{Combine SSUs and TSUs}\label{combine-ssus-and-tsus}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Combine all SSUs}
\NormalTok{all\_ssus }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{do.call}\NormalTok{(rbind, selected\_ssus)}

  \FunctionTok{mutate\_at}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{vars}\NormalTok{(PSU\_ID, SSU\_ID), as.numeric)}

\CommentTok{\# Combine all TSUs}
\NormalTok{all\_tsus }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{do.call}\NormalTok{(rbind, all\_psus\_tsus)}
\NormalTok{all\_tsus }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ all\_tsus }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate\_at}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{vars}\NormalTok{(PSU\_ID, SSU\_ID), as.numeric)}

\NormalTok{                    all\_ssus[}\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"PSU\_ID"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"SSU\_ID"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"SSU\_Type"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"replacement\_for"}\NormalTok{)])}

\CommentTok{\# Reorganize columns}
\NormalTok{all\_tsus }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ all\_tsus }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{PSU\_ID =}\NormalTok{ PSU\_ID.x, }
         \AttributeTok{SSU\_ID =}\NormalTok{ SSU\_ID.y, }
         \AttributeTok{SSU\_Type =}\NormalTok{ SSU\_Type.y,}
         \AttributeTok{Replacement\_for =}\NormalTok{ replacement\_for, }
\NormalTok{         TSU\_ID, }
\NormalTok{         geometry)}

\CommentTok{\# Label TSU types}

\NormalTok{all\_tsus}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{PSU\_Type }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"Target"}

\CommentTok{\# Final column selection}
\NormalTok{all\_tsus }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ all\_tsus }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
\NormalTok{  dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"PSU\_ID"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"SSU\_ID"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"SSU\_Type"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Replacement\_for"}\NormalTok{, }
                \StringTok{"TSU\_ID"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"TSU\_Type"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"geometry"}\NormalTok{)}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{✓ Total SSUs: \%d}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(all\_ssus)))}
\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"✓ Total TSUs: \%d}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(all\_tsus)))}
\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"✓ Target sampling sites: \%d}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }
            \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(all\_tsus}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{SSU\_Type }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Target"} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ all\_tsus}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{TSU\_Type }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Target"}\NormalTok{)))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsection{Compute Alternative PSUs}\label{alternative-psus}

Generate replacement PSUs from the same environmental clusters as targets.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Filter out already selected PSUs}
\NormalTok{remaining\_psus }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ all.PSU\_clusters }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{!}\NormalTok{(ID }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%}\NormalTok{ target.PSUs}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{ID))}

\CommentTok{\# Get unique cluster IDs from targets}
\NormalTok{unique\_clusters }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{unique}\NormalTok{(valid.PSU\_clusters}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Replace\_ID)}

\CommentTok{\# Initialize list for replacements}
\NormalTok{replacement\_psus }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{()}

\CommentTok{\# For each target cluster, select a replacement}
\ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ (clust\_id }\ControlFlowTok{in}\NormalTok{ unique\_clusters) \{}
  \CommentTok{\# Find candidates in same cluster}
\NormalTok{  candidates }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ remaining\_psus }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
    \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(cluster }\SpecialCharTok{==}\NormalTok{ clust\_id)}
  
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(candidates) }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{) \{}
    \CommentTok{\# Random selection from candidates}
\NormalTok{    replacement }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ candidates[}\FunctionTok{sample}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(candidates), }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{), ]}
\NormalTok{    replacement}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{replaces\_PSU }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ valid.PSU\_clusters}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{ID[}
\NormalTok{      valid.PSU\_clusters}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Replace\_ID }\SpecialCharTok{==}\NormalTok{ clust\_id}
\NormalTok{    ][}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]}
    
\NormalTok{    replacement\_psus }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rbind}\NormalTok{(replacement\_psus, replacement)}
\NormalTok{  \} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
    \FunctionTok{warning}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"No replacement found for cluster \%d"}\NormalTok{, clust\_id))}
\NormalTok{  \}}
\NormalTok{\}}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{✓ Generated \%d replacement PSUs}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(replacement\_psus)))}

\CommentTok{\# Export replacement PSUs}
\FunctionTok{write\_sf}\NormalTok{(replacement\_psus, }
         \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(results.path, }\StringTok{"/PSUs\_replacements.shp"}\NormalTok{), }
         \AttributeTok{overwrite =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{quote}
\textbf{Note}: Follow the same SSU and TSU generation process for replacement PSUs to create complete backup sampling locations.
\end{quote}

\subsection{Merging Results from Multiple Land Uses}\label{merging-results}

After running the sampling design separately for cropland, grassland, and forest, combine all results into a unified dataset with country-wide unique IDs.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\FunctionTok{library}\NormalTok{(data.table)}

\CommentTok{\# Define land uses and codes}
\NormalTok{landuses }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"cropland"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"grassland"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"forest"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{lu\_codes }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"C"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"G"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"F"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Initialize storage lists}
\NormalTok{psus\_target\_list }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{()}
\NormalTok{tsus\_target\_list }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{()}
\NormalTok{psus\_repl\_list }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{()}
\NormalTok{tsus\_repl\_list }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{()}

\CommentTok{\# Load all shapefiles}
\ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ (i }\ControlFlowTok{in} \FunctionTok{seq\_along}\NormalTok{(landuses)) \{}
\NormalTok{  lu }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ landuses[i]}
\NormalTok{  code }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ lu\_codes[i]}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Target PSUs}
\NormalTok{  file\_path }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"results/\%s/PSUs\_target.shp"}\NormalTok{, lu)}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{file.exists}\NormalTok{(file\_path)) \{}
\NormalTok{    temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{st\_read}\NormalTok{(file\_path, }\AttributeTok{quiet =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    temp}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{lulc }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ code}
\NormalTok{    psus\_target\_list[[lu]] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ temp}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"✓ Loaded \%s target PSUs (\%d)}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, lu, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(temp)))}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Target TSUs}
\NormalTok{  file\_path }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"results/\%s/TSUs\_target.shp"}\NormalTok{, lu)}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{file.exists}\NormalTok{(file\_path)) \{}
\NormalTok{    temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{st\_read}\NormalTok{(file\_path, }\AttributeTok{quiet =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    temp}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{lulc }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ code}
\NormalTok{    tsus\_target\_list[[lu]] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ temp}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"✓ Loaded \%s target TSUs (\%d)}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, lu, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(temp)))}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Replacement PSUs and TSUs}
  \CommentTok{\# (similar loading process)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\CommentTok{\# Merge using data.table (handles different column names)}

\subsection{Field Sampling Protocol}\label{field-protocol}

\subsubsection{GPS Device Preparation}\label{gps-prep}

\paragraph{Export to GPX Format}\label{export-to-gpx-format}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Load target TSUs}
\NormalTok{tsus\_field }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{st\_read}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"results/all/all\_tsus\_target.shp"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Filter to primary targets only (1 per SSU)}
\NormalTok{tsus\_field }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ tsus\_field }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(SSU\_Type }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Target"} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ TSU\_Type }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Target"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Transform to WGS84 (required for GPS)}
\NormalTok{tsus\_field\_wgs84 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{st\_transform}\NormalTok{(tsus\_field, }\AttributeTok{crs =} \DecValTok{4326}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Export to GPX}
\FunctionTok{st\_write}\NormalTok{(tsus\_field\_wgs84, }
         \StringTok{"results/all/field\_sampling\_points.gpx"}\NormalTok{, }
         \AttributeTok{driver =} \StringTok{"GPX"}\NormalTok{, }
         \AttributeTok{delete\_dsn =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}

\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"✓ Exported \%d waypoints to GPX}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(tsus\_field\_wgs84)))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\paragraph{Load onto GPS Device}\label{load-onto-gps-device}

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\tightlist
\item
  Connect GPS device to computer
\item
  Copy \texttt{field\_sampling\_points.gpx} to GPS memory
\item
  Load waypoints in GPS software
\item
  Waypoint names will be \texttt{site\_id} values (e.g., KEN0001-1-1C)
\end{enumerate}

\subsubsection{Sampling Procedure}\label{sampling-procedure}

\textbf{For each PSU (in order of PSU\_ID):}

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\item
  \textbf{Navigate to TSU 1} (SSU\_ID=1, TSU\_ID=1)

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    If accessible → Sample at exact GPS location
  \item
    If inaccessible (physical barrier) → Use TSU 2 (Alternative 1) or TSU 3 (Alternative 2)
  \end{itemize}
\item
  \textbf{Navigate to TSU 2} (SSU\_ID=2, TSU\_ID=1)

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    Repeat accessibility check and sampling
  \end{itemize}
\item
  \textbf{Navigate to TSU 3} (SSU\_ID=3, TSU\_ID=1)
\item
  \textbf{Navigate to TSU 4} (SSU\_ID=4, TSU\_ID=1)
\end{enumerate}

\textbf{If entire PSU is inaccessible:} - Use \texttt{replacement\_PSU\_ID} to find backup PSU - Navigate to replacement PSU location - Sample at replacement TSUs (SSU\_ID = 5, 6, 7, 8)

\subsubsection{Data Recording}\label{data-recording}

Field form should capture (Table \ref{tab:field-form}):

\begin{table}

\caption{\label{tab:field-form}Required field data recording}
\centering
\begin{tabular}[t]{l|l|l}
\hline
Field & Example & Notes\\
\hline
site\_id & KEN0001-1-1C & **CRITICAL** - Unique identifier\\
\hline
date & 2025-01-15 & Date of sampling\\
\hline
team & Team A & Field team name\\
\hline
coordinates\_actual & -1.2345, 36.7890 & Actual GPS coordinates\\
\hline
accessibility & Target / Alt1 / Alt2 & Which TSU was sampled\\
\hline
land\_use\_observed & Maize field & Visual confirmation\\
\hline
soil\_depth & 45 cm & Depth to restrictive layer\\
\hline
photos & KEN0001-1-1C\_001.jpg & Geotagged photos\\
\hline
notes & Rocky, 15\% slope & Relevant observations\\
\hline
\end{tabular}
\end{table}

\subsubsection{Quality Control}\label{qc}

\textbf{During field work:} - ✅ Verify land use matches expected type - ✅ Document if alternative TSU used (and reason) - ✅ Take geotagged photos at each site - ✅ Record actual GPS coordinates - ✅ Note any anomalies or challenges

\textbf{Post-field QC:} - Check for duplicate \texttt{site\_id} entries - Verify all mandatory fields completed - Cross-reference photos with field records - Flag sites with large GPS deviation (\textgreater30m from waypoint)

\section*{Appendix B: Troubleshooting Common Issues}\label{appendix-b-troubleshooting-common-issues}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Appendix B: Troubleshooting Common Issues}

\subsection{Memory Issues}\label{memory-issues}

\textbf{Problem}: R runs out of memory during processing

\textbf{Solution}:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Increase memory limit (Windows)}
\FunctionTok{memory.limit}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{size =} \DecValTok{32000}\NormalTok{)  }\CommentTok{\# 32 GB}

\CommentTok{\# Use terra instead of raster (more efficient)}
\CommentTok{\# Process data in chunks}
\CommentTok{\# Close unnecessary applications}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsection{CRS Misalignment}\label{crs-misalignment}

\textbf{Problem}: Spatial layers don't overlap correctly

\textbf{Solution}:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Always check CRS}
\NormalTok{sf}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{st\_crs}\NormalTok{(your\_data)}
\NormalTok{terra}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{crs}\NormalTok{(your\_raster)}

\CommentTok{\# Reproject if needed}
\NormalTok{your\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ sf}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{st\_transform}\NormalTok{(your\_data, }\AttributeTok{crs =}\NormalTok{ target\_crs)}
\NormalTok{your\_raster }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ terra}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{project}\NormalTok{(your\_raster, target\_crs)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsection{Empty Geometry}\label{empty-geometry}

\textbf{Problem}: SSU or TSU generation fails

\textbf{Solution}:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Check for valid geometries}
\FunctionTok{st\_is\_valid}\NormalTok{(your\_sf\_object)}

\CommentTok{\# Fix invalid geometries}
\NormalTok{your\_sf\_object }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{st\_make\_valid}\NormalTok{(your\_sf\_object)}

\CommentTok{\# Remove empty geometries}
\NormalTok{your\_sf\_object }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ your\_sf\_object[}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{st\_is\_empty}\NormalTok{(your\_sf\_object), ]}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}
